54 -CHASSIS ELECTRICAL > 54C-CONTROLLER AREA NETWORK (CAN) > TROUBLESHOOTING<CAN> > CAN BUS DIAGNOSIS > DIAGNOSIS ITEM 22
Diagnosis Item 22: Diagnose when the M.U.T.-III cannot receive the data sent by emergency call control unit. <Vehicles with ERA-GLONASS system>
 
 
cautionWhen servicing a CAN bus line, earth yourself by touching a metal object such as an unpainted water pipe. If you fail to do, a component connected to the CAN bus line may be broken.
 
 
FUNCTION
The diagnostic result demonstrates that "the M.U.T.-III cannot receive the sent data from the emergency call control unit" when the M.U.T.-III checks the periodically sent data from each ECU and cannot receive the emergency call control unit data only.
 
 
TROUBLE JUDGEMENT CONDITIONS
M.U.T.-III judges the trouble when the periodically sent data from the emergency call control unit cannot be received.
 
 
PROBABLE CAUSES
  • Damaged harness wires and connectors
  • Power supply circuit malfunction of the emergency call control unit
  • Malfunction of the emergency call control unit
 
 
DIAGNOSIS PROCEDURE
STEP 1. Connector check: joint connector (CAN2) and emergency call control unit connector
cautionThe strand end of the twist wire should be within 10 cm from the connector.
When checking the joint connector, ensure that its wiring harness side and its short pins are not damaged.
Is the check result normal?
Go to Step 2.
Repair the defective connector. Replace the joint connector as necessary.
 
STEP 2. Resistance measurement at joint connector (CAN2) and emergency call control unit connector
caution
  • A digital multimeter should be used.
  • The test wiring harness should be used.
  • When measuring the resistance, disconnect the negative battery terminal.
  • Strictly observe the specified wiring harness repair procedure.
(1) Disconnect joint connector (CAN2) and the emergency call control unit connector, and measure at the wiring harness side.
(2) Turn the ignition switch to the "LOCK" (OFF) position.
(3) Ensure that the negative battery terminal is disconnected.
(4) Continuity between joint connector (CAN2) terminal No. 1 and emergency call control unit connector terminal No. 25
OK: Continuity (2 Ω or less)
(5) Continuity between joint connector (CAN2) terminal No. 12 and emergency call control unit connector terminal No. 24
OK: Continuity (2 Ω or less)
Is the check result normal?
<All the resistances measure 2 Ω or less> Power supply to the emergency call control unit may be suspected. Troubleshoot the ERA-GLONASS system (Refer to GROUP 54A - ERA-GLONASS System, Troubleshooting ).
NO : <Either or all of the resistances measure more than 2 Ω> Repair the wiring harness between joint connector (CAN2) and the emergency call control unit connector.
 
 
54 -CHASSIS ELECTRICAL > 54C-CONTROLLER AREA NETWORK (CAN) > TROUBLESHOOTING<CAN> > CAN BUS DIAGNOSIS > DIAGNOSIS ITEM 23
Diagnosis Item 23: Diagnose when the M.U.T.-III cannot receive the data sent by ASTC-ECU.
 
 
cautionWhen servicing a CAN bus line, earth yourself by touching a metal object such as an unpainted water pipe. If you fail to do, a component connected to the CAN bus line may be broken.
 
 
FUNCTION
The diagnostic result demonstrates that "the M.U.T.-III cannot receive the sent data from the ASTC-ECU" when the M.U.T.-III checks the periodically sent data from each ECU and cannot receive the ASTC-ECU data only.
 
 
TROUBLE JUDGEMENT CONDITIONS
M.U.T.-III judges the trouble when the periodically sent data from the ASTC-ECU cannot be received.
 
 
PROBABLE CAUSES
  • Damaged harness wires and connectors
  • Power supply circuit malfunction of the ASTC-ECU
  • Malfunction of the ASTC-ECU
 
 
DIAGNOSIS PROCEDURE
STEP 1. Connector check: joint connector (CAN2) and ASTC-ECU connector
cautionThe strand end of the twist wire should be within 10 cm from the connector.
When checking the joint connector, ensure that its wiring harness side and its short pins are not damaged.
Is the check result normal?
Go to Step 2.
Repair the defective connector. Replace the joint connector as necessary.
 
STEP 2. Resistance measurement at joint connector (CAN2) and ASTC-ECU connector
caution
  • A digital multimeter should be used.
  • The test wiring harness should be used.
  • When measuring the resistance, disconnect the negative battery terminal.
  • Strictly observe the specified wiring harness repair procedure.
(1) Disconnect joint connector (CAN2) and the ASTC-ECU connector, and measure at the wiring harness side.
(2) Turn the ignition switch to the "LOCK" (OFF) position.
(3) Ensure that the negative battery terminal is disconnected.
(4) Continuity between joint connector (CAN2) terminal No. 5 and ASTC-ECU connector terminal No. 16 <LHD>
OK: Continuity (2 Ω or less)
(5) Continuity between joint connector (CAN2) terminal No. 16 and ASTC-ECU connector terminal No. 4 <LHD>
OK: Continuity (2 Ω or less)
(6) Continuity between joint connector (CAN2) terminal No. 3 and ASTC-ECU connector terminal No. 16 <RHD>
OK: Continuity (2 Ω or less)
(7) Continuity between joint connector (CAN2) terminal No. 14 and ASTC-ECU connector terminal No. 4 <RHD>
OK: Continuity (2 Ω or less)
Is the check result normal?
<All the resistances measure 2 Ω or less> Power supply to the ASTC-ECU may be suspected. Troubleshoot the ASTC (Refer to GROUP 35C - Troubleshooting ).
NO : <Either or all of the resistances measure more than 2 Ω> Check the intermediate connector, and repair if necessary. If the intermediate connector is in good condition, repair the wiring harness between joint connector (CAN2) and the ASTC-ECU connector.
 
 
54 -CHASSIS ELECTRICAL > 54C-CONTROLLER AREA NETWORK (CAN) > TROUBLESHOOTING<CAN> > CAN BUS DIAGNOSIS > DIAGNOSIS ITEM 24
Diagnosis Item 24: Diagnose when the M.U.T.-III cannot receive the data sent by AS&G-ECU. <Vehicles with AS&G system>
 
 
cautionWhen servicing a CAN bus line, earth yourself by touching a metal object such as an unpainted water pipe. If you fail to do, a component connected to the CAN bus line may be broken.
 
 
FUNCTION
The diagnostic result demonstrates that "the M.U.T.-III cannot receive the sent data from the steering wheel sensor" when the M.U.T.-III checks the periodically sent data from each ECU and cannot receive the steering wheel sensor data only.
 
 
TROUBLE JUDGEMENT CONDITIONS
M.U.T.-III judges the trouble when the periodically sent data from AS&G-ECU cannot be received.
 
 
PROBABLE CAUSES
  • Damaged harness wires and connectors
  • Power supply circuit malfunction of the AS&G-ECU
  • Malfunction of the AS&G-ECU
 
 
DIAGNOSIS PROCEDURE
STEP 1. Connector check: joint connector (CAN1) <LHD> or joint connector (CAN2) <RHD> and AS&G-ECU connector
cautionThe strand end of the twist wire should be within 10 cm from the connector.
When checking the joint connector, ensure that its wiring harness side and its short pins are not damaged.
Is the check result normal?
Go to Step 2.
Repair the defective connector. Replace the joint connector as necessary.
 
STEP 2. Resistance measurement at joint connector (CAN1) <LHD> or joint connector (CAN2) <RHD> and AS&G-ECU connector
caution
  • A digital multimeter should be used.
  • The test wiring harness should be used.
  • When measuring the resistance, disconnect the negative battery terminal.
  • Strictly observe the specified wiring harness repair procedure.
(1) Disconnect joint connector (CAN1) <LHD> or joint connector (CAN2) <RHD> and the AS&G-ECU connector, and measure at the wiring harness side.
(2) Turn the ignition switch to the "LOCK" (OFF) position.
(3) Ensure that the negative battery terminal is disconnected.
(4) Continuity between joint connector (CAN1) terminal No. 8 and AS&G-ECU connector terminal No. 1 <LHD>
OK: Continuity (2 Ω or less)
(5) Continuity between joint connector (CAN1) terminal No. 19 and AS&G-ECU connector terminal No. 14 <LHD>
OK: Continuity (2 Ω or less)
(6) Continuity between joint connector (CAN2) terminal No. 2 and AS&G-ECU connector terminal No. 1 <RHD>
OK: Continuity (2 Ω or less)
(7) Continuity between joint connector (CAN2) terminal No. 13 and AS&G-ECU connector terminal No. 14 <RHD>
OK: Continuity (2 Ω or less)
Is the check result normal?
<All the resistances measure 2 Ω or less> Power supply to the steering wheel sensor may be suspected. Diagnose the AS&G-ECU (Refer to GROUP 17 - AS&G System, Troubleshooting <M/T> or <A/T>).
NO : <Either or all of the resistances measure more than 2 Ω> Repair the wiring harness between joint connector (CAN1) <LHD> or joint connector (CAN2) <RHD> and the AS&G-ECU.
 
 
54 -CHASSIS ELECTRICAL > 54C-CONTROLLER AREA NETWORK (CAN) > TROUBLESHOOTING<CAN> > CAN BUS DIAGNOSIS > DIAGNOSIS ITEM 25
Diagnosis Item 25: Diagnose when the M.U.T.-III cannot receive the data sent by engine-ECU.
 
 
cautionWhen servicing a CAN bus line, earth yourself by touching a metal object such as an unpainted water pipe. If you fail to do, a component connected to the CAN bus line may be broken.
 
 
FUNCTION
The diagnostic result demonstrates that "the M.U.T.-III cannot receive the sent data from the engine-ECU" when the M.U.T.-III checks the periodically sent data from each ECU and cannot receive the engine-ECU data only.
 
 
TROUBLE JUDGEMENT CONDITIONS
M.U.T.-III judges the trouble when the periodically sent data from engine-ECU cannot be received.
 
 
PROBABLE CAUSES
  • Damaged harness wires and connectors
  • Power supply circuit malfunction of the engine-ECU
  • Malfunction of the engine-ECU
 
 
DIAGNOSIS PROCEDURE
STEP 1. Connector check: joint connector (CAN2) and engine-ECU connector
cautionThe strand end of the twist wire should be within 10 cm from the connector.
When checking the joint connector, ensure that its wiring harness side and its short pins are not damaged.
Is the check result normal?
Go to Step 2.
Repair the defective connector. Replace the joint connector as necessary.
 
STEP 2. Resistance measurement at joint connector (CAN2) and engine-ECU connector
caution
  • A digital multimeter should be used.
  • The test wiring harness should be used.
  • When measuring the resistance, disconnect the negative battery terminal.
  • Strictly observe the specified wiring harness repair procedure.
(1) Disconnect the joint connector (CAN2) and the engine-ECU connector, and measure at the wiring harness side.
(2) Turn the ignition switch to the "LOCK" (OFF) position.
(3) Ensure that the negative battery terminal is disconnected.
(4) Continuity between joint connector (CAN2) terminal No. 10 and engine-ECU connector terminal No. 153 <4N14 (LHD)>
OK: Continuity (2 Ω or less)
(5) Continuity between joint connector (CAN2) terminal No. 21 and engine-ECU connector terminal No. 166 <4N14 (LHD)>
OK: Continuity (2 Ω or less)
(6) Continuity between joint connector (CAN2) terminal No. 10 and engine-ECU connector terminal No. 108 <4N15 (LHD)>
OK: Continuity (2 Ω or less)
(7) Continuity between joint connector (CAN2) terminal No. 21 and engine-ECU connector terminal No. 109 <4N15 (LHD)>
OK: Continuity (2 Ω or less)
(8) Continuity between joint connector (CAN2) terminal No. 11 and engine-ECU connector terminal No. 153 <RHD>
OK: Continuity (2 Ω or less)
(9) Continuity between joint connector (CAN2) terminal No. 22 and engine-ECU connector terminal No. 166 <RHD>
OK: Continuity (2 Ω or less)
Is the check result normal?
<All the resistances measure 2 Ω or less> Go to Step 3 .
NO : <Either or all of the resistances measure more than 2 Ω> Check the intermediate connector, and repair if necessary. If the intermediate connector is in good condition, repair the wiring harness between joint connector (CAN2) and the engine-ECU.
 
STEP 3. Resistance measurement at engine-ECU connector.
caution
  • A digital multimeter should be used.
  • Strictly observe the specified wiring harness repair procedure.
(1) Remove the engine-ECU, and measure at the equipment side.
(2) Resistance between engine-ECU connector terminal Nos.153 and 166 <4N14>
OK: 120 ± 20 Ω
(3) Resistance between engine-ECU connector terminal Nos.108 and 109 <4N15>
OK: 120 ± 20 Ω
Is the check result normal?
<Within 120 ± 20 Ω> Power supply to the engine-ECU may be suspected. Troubleshoot the engine system (Refer to GROUP 13A - Troubleshooting ).
<Not within 120 ± 20 Ω> Replace the engine-ECU (Refer to GROUP 13A - Engine-ECU <4N14> or <4N15>).
 
 
54 -CHASSIS ELECTRICAL > 54C-CONTROLLER AREA NETWORK (CAN) > TROUBLESHOOTING<CAN> > CAN BUS DIAGNOSIS > DIAGNOSIS ITEM 26
Diagnosis Item 26: Diagnose when the M.U.T.-III cannot receive the data sent by Dosing Control Unit (DCU). <4N14>
 
 
cautionWhen servicing a CAN bus line, earth yourself by touching a metal object such as an unpainted water pipe. If you fail to do, a component connected to the CAN bus line may be broken.
 
 
FUNCTION
The diagnostic result demonstrates that "the M.U.T.-III cannot receive the sent data from the DCU" when the M.U.T.-III checks the periodically sent data from each ECU and cannot receive the DCU data only.
 
 
TROUBLE JUDGEMENT CONDITIONS
M.U.T.-III judges the trouble when the periodically sent data from DCU cannot be received.
 
 
PROBABLE CAUSES
  • Damaged harness wires and connectors
  • Power supply circuit malfunction of the DCU
  • Malfunction of the DCU
  • Malfunction of the engine-ECU
 
 
DIAGNOSIS PROCEDURE
STEP 1. Connector check: joint connector (CAN4), engine-ECU connector and DCU connector
cautionThe strand end of the twist wire should be within 10 cm from the connector.
Is the check result normal?
Go to Step 2.
Repair the defective connector. Replace the joint connector as necessary.
 
STEP 2. Resistance measurement at joint connector (CAN4) and DCU connector.
caution
  • A digital multimeter should be used.
  • The test wiring harness should be used.
  • When measuring the resistance, disconnect the negative battery terminal.
  • Strictly observe the specified wiring harness repair procedure.
(1) Disconnect the joint connector (CAN4) and the DCU connector, and measure at the wiring harness side.
(2) Turn the ignition switch to the "LOCK" (OFF) position.
(3) Ensure that the negative battery terminal is disconnected.
(4) Continuity between joint connector (CAN4) terminal No. 10 and DCU connector terminal No. 87
OK: Continuity (2 Ω or less)
(5) Continuity between joint connector (CAN4) terminal No. 21 and DCU connector terminal No. 65
OK: Continuity (2 Ω or less)
Is the check result normal?
<All the resistances measure 2 Ω or less> Go to Step 3 .
NO : <Either or all of the resistances measure more than 2 Ω> Check intermediate connector, and repair if necessary. If the intermediate connector is in good condition, repair the wiring harness between joint connector (CAN4) and the DCU connector.
 
STEP 3. Resistance measurement at joint connector (CAN4) and engine-ECU connector.
caution
  • A digital multimeter should be used.
  • The test wiring harness should be used.
  • When measuring the resistance, disconnect the negative battery terminal.
  • Strictly observe the specified wiring harness repair procedure.
(1) Disconnect the joint connector (CAN4) and engine-ECU connector, and measure at the wiring harness side.
(2) Turn the ignition switch to the "LOCK" (OFF) position.
(3) Ensure that the negative battery terminal is disconnected.
(4) Continuity between joint connector (CAN4) terminal No. 11 and engine-ECU connector terminal No. 74
OK: Continuity (2 Ω or less)
(5) Continuity between joint connector (CAN4) terminal No. 22 and engine-ECU connector terminal No. 75
OK: Continuity (2 Ω or less)
Is the check result normal?
<All the resistances measure 2 Ω or less> Go to Step 4 .
NO : <Either or all of the resistances measure more than 2 Ω> Repair the wiring harness between joint connector (CAN4) and the engine-ECU connector.
 
STEP 4. Resistance measurement at engine-ECU connector.
cautionA digital multimeter should be used.
(1) Remove the engine-ECU, and measure at the equipment side.
(2) Resistance at engine-ECU connector terminal Nos. 74 and 75
OK: 120 ± 20 Ω
Is the check result normal?
<Within 120 ± 20 Ω> Go to Step 5.
<Not within 120 ± 20 Ω> Replace the engine-ECU (Refer to GROUP 13A - Engine-ECU <4N14> or <4N15>).
 
STEP 5. Resistance measurement at DCU connector.
cautionA digital multimeter should be used.
(1) Remove the DCU, and measure at the equipment side.
(2) Resistance at DCU connector terminal Nos. 87 and 65
OK: 120 ± 20 Ω
Is the check result normal?
<Within 120 ± 20 Ω> The trouble can be an intermittent malfunction (Refer to GROUP 00 - How to Cope with Intermittent Malfunction ).
<Not within 120 ± 20 Ω> Replace the DCU.

54 -CHASSIS ELECTRICAL > 54C-CONTROLLER AREA NETWORK (CAN) > TROUBLESHOOTING<GATEWAY-ECU (FOR GW-CAN-C)> > DIAGNOSIS FUNCTION
DIAGNOSIS FUNCTION
 
 
HOW TO READ DIAGNOSIS CODE
Use the M.U.T.-III to read diagnosis code (Refer to GROUP 00 - Diagnosis Function ).
 
 
 
HOW TO ERASING DIAGNOSIS CODE
Use the M.U.T.-III to erasing diagnosis code (Refer to GROUP 00 - Diagnosis Function ).
 
 
 
CHECK OF FREEZE FRAME DATA
To detect fault and set the diagnosis code, the gateway-ECU (for GW-CAN-C) obtains data before the confirmation of the diagnosis code and data when the diagnosis code is confirmed, and then stores the current condition of the gateway-ECU (for GW-CAN-C). By analysing each data from M.U.T.-III, the troubleshooting can be performed more efficiently. Display items of the freeze frame data are as follows.
 
 
Display item list
Item No.Item nameData itemUnit
1OdometerTotal driving distance after the diagnosis code is generatedkm
2Ignition cycleNumber of times the ignition switch is turned "ON" or "LOCK" (OFF) after the past failure transition.Number of counts is displayed.
4Accumulated minuteCumulative time for current malfunction of diagnosis codemin
 
54 -CHASSIS ELECTRICAL > 54C-CONTROLLER AREA NETWORK (CAN) > TROUBLESHOOTING<GATEWAY-ECU (FOR GW-CAN-C)> > DIAGNOSIS CODE CHART
DIAGNOSIS CODE CHART
cautionDuring troubleshooting, a diagnosis code associated with other systems may be set when the ignition switch is turned "ON" with connector(s) disconnected. On the completion of troubleshooting, confirm all systems for diagnosis code(s). If diagnosis code(s) are set, erase them all.
Diagnosis code No.Diagnostic itemReference page
B1083EEPROM fail
U0141ETACS CAN timeout

54 -CHASSIS ELECTRICAL > 54C-CONTROLLER AREA NETWORK (CAN) > TROUBLESHOOTING<GATEWAY-ECU (FOR GW-CAN-C)> > DIAGNOSIS CODE PROCEDURES > CODE No.B1083 EEPROM FAIL
Code No. B1083: EEPROM Fail
 
 
 
 
TROUBLE JUDGEMENT
If at least 1 error occurs while the gateway-ECU (for GW-CAN-C) sends data to and receives from the EEPROM, the gateway-ECU (for GW-CAN-C) sets diagnosis code No. B1083.
 
 
PROBABLE CAUSE
  • Malfunction of the gateway-ECU (for GW-CAN-C)
54 -CHASSIS ELECTRICAL > 54C-CONTROLLER AREA NETWORK (CAN) > TROUBLESHOOTING<GATEWAY-ECU (FOR GW-CAN-C)> > DIAGNOSIS CODE PROCEDURES > CODE No.U0141 ETACS CAN TIMEOUT
Code No. U0141: ETACS CAN Timeout
 
 
caution
  • If diagnosis code No. U0141 is set, be sure to diagnose the CAN bus line.
  • When replacing the ECU, always check that the communication circuit is normal.
 
 
TROUBLE JUDGEMENT
If the signal from ETACS-ECU cannot be received, the gateway-ECU (for GW-CAN-C) sets diagnosis code No. U0141.
 
 
JUDGEMENT CRITERIA
With the ignition switch is at "ON" position, diagnosis code No. U1190 is not set, if the communication with ETACS-ECU cannot be established for 2,500 ms or more, the gateway-ECU (for GW-CAN-C) determines that a problem has occurred.
 
 
PROBABLE CAUSES
  • Malfunction of CAN bus line
  • Malfunction of the gateway-ECU (for GW-CAN-C)
  • Malfunction of the ETACS-ECU
 
 
DIAGNOSIS PROCEDURE
STEP 1. M.U.T.-III CAN bus diagnostics
Use the M.U.T.-III to diagnose the CAN bus lines.
Is the check result normal?
Go to Step 2.
Repair the CAN bus line (Refer to ).
 
STEP 2. M.U.T.-III other system diagnosis code
Check that the other ECU, which belongs to the CAN-C (main) bus line and performs CAN communication with the ETACS-ECU, sets diagnosis code No. U0141 (Refer to ).
Is the diagnosis code set?
Go to Step 3.
Go to Step 4.
 
STEP 3. Check whether the diagnosis code is set again.
Recheck if the diagnosis code is set.
(1) Erase the diagnosis code.
(2) Turn the ignition switch from "LOCK" (OFF) position to "ON" position.
(3) On completion, check that the diagnosis code is not set again.
Is the diagnosis code set?
Replace ETACS-ECU (Refer to GROUP 54A - ETACS ).
A poor connection, open circuit or other intermittent malfunction is present in the CAN bus lines between the ETACS-ECU and the gateway-ECU (for GW-CAN-C) (Refer to GROUP 00 - How to Cope with Intermittent Malfunctions ).
 
STEP 4. Check whether the diagnosis code is set again.
Recheck if the diagnosis code is set.
(1) Erase the diagnosis code.
(2) Turn the ignition switch from "LOCK" (OFF) position to "ON" position.
(3) On completion, check that the diagnosis code is not set again.
Is the diagnosis code set?
Replace gateway-ECU (for GW-CAN-C) (Refer to ).
A poor connection, open circuit or other intermittent malfunction is present in the CAN bus lines between the ETACS-ECU and the gateway-ECU (for GW-CAN-C) (Refer to GROUP 00 - How to Cope with Intermittent Malfunctions ).
 
54 -CHASSIS ELECTRICAL > 54C-CONTROLLER AREA NETWORK (CAN) > TROUBLESHOOTING<GATEWAY-ECU (FOR GW-CAN-C)> > DIAGNOSIS CODE PROCEDURES > CODE No.U0155 METER CAN TIMEOUT
Code No. U0155: Meter CAN Timeout
 
 
caution
  • If diagnosis code No. U0155 is set, be sure to diagnose the CAN bus line.
  • When replacing the ECU, always check that the communication circuit is normal.
 
 
TROUBLE JUDGEMENT
If signal from the combination meter cannot be received for 2,500 ms or more, the gateway-ECU (for GW-CAN-C) sets diagnosis code No. U0155.

  • Malfunction of the gateway-ECU (for GW-CAN-C)

Use the M.U.T.-III to diagnose the CAN bus lines.
Is the check result normal?
Go to Step 2.
Repair the CAN bus line (Refer to ).
 
STEP 2. M.U.T.-III other system diagnosis code
Check that the other ECU, which belongs to the CAN-C (main) bus line and performs CAN communication with the combination meter, sets diagnosis code No. U0155 (Refer to ).
Is the diagnosis code set?
Go to Step 3.
Go to Step 4.
 
STEP 3. Check whether the diagnosis code is set again.
Check again if the diagnosis code is set in the gateway-ECU (for GW-CAN-C).
(1) Erase the diagnosis code.
(2) Turn the ignition switch from "LOCK" (OFF) position to "ON" position.
(3) On completion, check that the diagnosis code is set again.
Is the diagnosis code set?
Replace the combination meter (Refer to GROUP 54A - Combination Meter ).
A poor connection, open circuit or other intermittent malfunction is present in the CAN bus lines between the combination meter and the gateway-ECU (for GW-CAN-C) (Refer to GROUP 00 - How to Cope with Intermittent Malfunctions ).
 
STEP 4. Check whether the diagnosis code is set again.
Check again if the diagnosis code is set in the gateway-ECU (for GW-CAN-C).
(1) Erase the diagnosis code.
(2) Turn the ignition switch from "LOCK" (OFF) position to "ON" position.
(3) On completion, check that the diagnosis code is not set again.
Is the diagnosis code set?
Replace the gateway-ECU (for GW-CAN-C) (Refer to ).
A poor connection, open circuit or other intermittent malfunction is present in the CAN bus lines between the combination meter and the gateway-ECU (for GW-CAN-C) (Refer to GROUP 00 - How to Cope with Intermittent Malfunctions ).
 
54 -CHASSIS ELECTRICAL > 54C-CONTROLLER AREA NETWORK (CAN) > TROUBLESHOOTING<GATEWAY-ECU (FOR GW-CAN-C)> > DIAGNOSIS CODE PROCEDURES > CODE No.U1073 BUS-OFF
Code No. U1073: Bus-off (GW-CAN-C)
 
 
caution
  • If diagnosis code No. U0173 is set, be sure to diagnose the CAN bus line.
  • When replacing the ECU, always check that the communication circuit is normal.
 
 
TROUBLE JUDGEMENT
When gateway-ECU (for GW-CAN-C) has ceased the CAN (GW-CAN-C) communication (bus off), code No. U1073 is set.
 
 
PROBABLE CAUSES
  • Malfunction of CAN bus line
  • Malfunction of the gateway-ECU (for GW-CAN-C)
  • ECU malfunction of other system
54 -CHASSIS ELECTRICAL > 54C-CONTROLLER AREA NETWORK (CAN) > TROUBLESHOOTING<GATEWAY-ECU (FOR GW-CAN-C)> > DIAGNOSIS CODE PROCEDURES > CODE No.U1190 NO RECEIVE FAULT DETECT SIGNAL
Code No. U1190: No receive fault detect signal
 
 
caution
  • If diagnosis code No. U1190 is set, be sure to diagnose the CAN bus line.
  • When replacing the ECU, always check that the communication circuit is normal.
 
 
JUDGEMENT CRITERIA
ETACS-ECU sends the diagnosis code (U code) detection permission or prohibition signal to each ECU connected to the CAN bus line. If the gateway-ECU (for GW-CAN-C) cannot receive the diagnosis code (U code) detection permission or prohibition signal for 5 seconds after turning the ignition switch to "ON" position, diagnosis code No. U1190 will be set.
 
 
PROBABLE CAUSES
  • Malfunction of the ETACS-ECU
  • Malfunction of CAN bus line
  • Malfunction of the gateway-ECU (for GW-CAN-C)
 
 
DIAGNOSIS PROCEDURE
STEP 1. M.U.T.-III CAN bus diagnostics
Use the M.U.T.-III to diagnose the CAN bus lines.
Is the check result normal?
Go to Step 2.
Repair the CAN bus line (Refer to ).
 
STEP 2. M.U.T.-III other system diagnosis code
Check if the diagnosis code is set in the combination meter.
Is the diagnosis code set?
Replace the ETACS-ECU (Refer to GROUP 54A - ETACS ).
Go to Step 3.
 
STEP 3. Diagnosis code recheck
Check again if the diagnosis code is set in the gateway-ECU (for GW-CAN-C).
(1) Erase the diagnosis code.
(2) Turn the ignition switch from "LOCK" (OFF) position to "ON" position.
(3) Check if the diagnosis code is set.
Is the diagnosis code set?
Replace the gateway-ECU (for GW-CAN-C) (Refer to ).
Intermittent malfunction is suspected (Refer to GROUP 00 - How to cope with Intermittent Malfunction ).

54 -CHASSIS ELECTRICAL > 54C-CONTROLLER AREA NETWORK (CAN) > TROUBLESHOOTING<GATEWAY-ECU (FOR GW-CAN-C)> > SYMPTOM CHART

54 -CHASSIS ELECTRICAL > 54C-CONTROLLER AREA NETWORK (CAN) > TROUBLESHOOTING<GATEWAY-ECU (FOR GW-CAN-C)> > SYMPTOM PROCEDURE > POWER SUPPLY CIRCUIT
Inspection Procedure 1: Power Supply Circuit Check
 
 
 
 
COMMENTS ON TROUBLE SYMPTOM
If the gateway-ECU (for GW-CAN-C) functions do not work at all, power supply to the gateway-ECU (for GW-CAN-C), or the gateway-ECU (for GW-CAN-C) itself may have a problem.
 
 
PROBABLE CAUSES
  • Damaged harness wires and connectors
  • Malfunction of gateway-ECU (for GW-CAN-C)
 
 
DIAGNOSIS PROCEDURE
STEP 1. Voltage measurement at the gateway-ECU (for GW-CAN-C) connector
(1) Disconnect the connector, and measure at the wiring harness side.
(2) Turn the ignition switch to the "LOCK" (OFF) position.
(3) Measure the voltage between the gateway-ECU (for GW-CAN-C) connector (+B terminal) and the body earth.
OK: System voltage
Is the check result normal?
Go to Step 3.
Go to Step 2.
 
STEP 2. Check of open circuit in +B line between the fusible link and gateway-ECU (for GW-CAN-C) connector
Is the check result normal?
Perform the battery test (Refer to GROUP 54A - Battery, Battery Test ) or check the battery terminals for looseness or contamination.
Repair the connector(s) or wiring harness.
 
STEP 3. Voltage measurement at the gateway-ECU (for GW-CAN-C) connector
(1) Disconnect the connector, and measure at the wiring harness side.
(2) Turn the ignition switch to the "ON" position.
(3) Measure the voltage between the gateway-ECU (for GW-CAN-C) connector (IG terminal) and the body earth.
OK: System voltage
Is the check result normal?
Go to Step 6.
Go to Step 4.
 
STEP 4. M.U.T.-III other system data list
Check the input signal from the ignition switch (IG1) in the ETACS-ECU.
  • Turn the ignition switch to the "ON" position.
 
Item No.Item nameNormal condition
30IG SW (IG1)ON
OK: Normal condition is displayed.
Is the check result normal?
Go to Step 5.
NO : Troubleshoot the ETACS-ECU (Refer to GROUP 54A - ETACS, Inspection Procedure 2 "The ignition switch (IG1) signal is not received." ).
 
STEP 5. Check of open circuit in IG line between the ignition switch (IG1) and gateway-ECU (for GW-CAN-C) connector
Is the check result normal?
The trouble can be an intermittent malfunction (Refer to GROUP 00 - How to Cope with Intermittent Malfunction ).
Repair the connector(s) or wiring harness.
 
STEP 6. Resistance measurement at the gateway-ECU (for GW-CAN-C) connector
(1) Disconnect the connector, and measure at the wiring harness side.
(2) Measure the resistance between the gateway-ECU (for GW-CAN-C) connector (GND terminal) and the body earth.
OK: Continuity exists (2 Ω or less)
Is the check result normal?
Go to Step 8.
Go to Step 7.
 
STEP 7. Check of open circuit in GND line between gateway-ECU (for GW-CAN-C) connector and body earth
Is the check result normal?
The trouble can be an intermittent malfunction (Refer to GROUP 00 - How to Cope with Intermittent Malfunction ).
Repair the connector(s) or wiring harness.
 
STEP 8. Retest the system.
Is the check result normal?
The trouble can be an intermittent malfunction (Refer to GROUP 00 - How to Cope with Intermittent Malfunction ).
Replace the gateway-ECU (for GW-CAN-C) (Refer to ).

cautionWhenever the ECU is replaced, ensure that the input signal circuit is normal.

  • Damaged harness wires and connectors

Is the check result normal?
Go to Step 3.
Repair the connector(s) or wiring harness.

54 -CHASSIS ELECTRICAL > 54C-CONTROLLER AREA NETWORK (CAN) > TROUBLESHOOTING<GATEWAY-ECU (FOR BSW)> > DIAGNOSIS CODE PROCEDURES > CODE No.U0141 ETACS CAN TIMEOUT
Code No. U0141: ETACS CAN Timeout
 
 
caution
  • If diagnosis code No. U0141 is set, be sure to diagnose the CAN bus line.
  • When replacing the ECU, always check that the communication circuit is normal.
 
 
TROUBLE JUDGEMENT
If the signal from ETACS-ECU cannot be received, the gateway-ECU (for BSW) sets diagnosis code No. U0141.
 
 
JUDGEMENT CRITERIA
With the ignition switch is at "ON" position, diagnosis code No. U1190 is not set, if the communication with ETACS-ECU cannot be established for 2,500 ms or more, the gateway-ECU (for BSW) determines that a problem has occurred.
 
 
PROBABLE CAUSES
  • Malfunction of CAN bus line
  • Malfunction of the gateway-ECU (for BSW)
  • Malfunction of the ETACS-ECU
 
 
DIAGNOSIS PROCEDURE
STEP 1. M.U.T.-III CAN bus diagnostics
Use the M.U.T.-III to diagnose the CAN bus lines.
Is the check result normal?
Go to Step 2.
Repair the CAN bus line (Refer to ).
 
STEP 2. M.U.T.-III other system diagnosis code
Check that the other ECU, which belongs to the CAN-C (main) bus line and performs CAN communication with the ETACS-ECU, sets diagnosis code No. U0141 (Refer to ).
Is the diagnosis code set?
Go to Step 3.
Go to Step 4.
 
STEP 3. Check whether the diagnosis code is set again.
Recheck if the diagnosis code is set.
(1) Erase the diagnosis code.
(2) Turn the ignition switch from "LOCK" (OFF) position to "ON" position.
(3) On completion, check that the diagnosis code is not set again.
Is the diagnosis code set?
Replace ETACS-ECU (Refer to GROUP 54A - ETACS ).
A poor connection, open circuit or other intermittent malfunction is present in the CAN bus lines between the ETACS-ECU and the gateway-ECU (for BSW) (Refer to GROUP 00 - How to Cope with Intermittent Malfunctions ).
 
STEP 4. Check whether the diagnosis code is set again.
Recheck if the diagnosis code is set.
(1) Erase the diagnosis code.
(2) Turn the ignition switch from "LOCK" (OFF) position to "ON" position.
(3) On completion, check that the diagnosis code is not set again.
Is the diagnosis code set?
Replace gateway-ECU (for BSW) (Refer to ).
A poor connection, open circuit or other intermittent malfunction is present in the CAN bus lines between the ETACS-ECU and the gateway-ECU (for BSW) (Refer to GROUP 00 - How to Cope with Intermittent Malfunctions ).
 
54 -CHASSIS ELECTRICAL > 54C-CONTROLLER AREA NETWORK (CAN) > TROUBLESHOOTING<GATEWAY-ECU (FOR BSW)> > DIAGNOSIS CODE PROCEDURES > CODE No.U0155 METER CAN TIMEOUT
Code No. U0155: Meter CAN Timeout
 
 
caution
  • If diagnosis code No. U0155 is set, be sure to diagnose the CAN bus line.
  • When replacing the ECU, always check that the communication circuit is normal.
 
 
TROUBLE JUDGEMENT
If signal from the combination meter cannot be received for 2,500 ms or more, the gateway-ECU (for BSW) sets diagnosis code No. U0155.

  • Malfunction of CAN bus line
  • Malfunction of the combination meter
  • Malfunction of the gateway-ECU (for BSW)
 
 
DIAGNOSIS PROCEDURE
STEP 1. M.U.T.-III CAN bus diagnostics
Use the M.U.T.-III to diagnose the CAN bus lines.
Is the check result normal?
Go to Step 2.
Repair the CAN bus line (Refer to ).
 
STEP 2. M.U.T.-III other system diagnosis code
Check that the other ECU, which belongs to the CAN-C (main) bus line and performs CAN communication with the combination meter, sets diagnosis code No. U0155 (Refer to ).
Is the diagnosis code set?
Go to Step 3.
Go to Step 4.
 
STEP 3. Check whether the diagnosis code is set again.
Check again if the diagnosis code is set in the gateway-ECU (for BSW).
(1) Erase the diagnosis code.
(2) Turn the ignition switch from "LOCK" (OFF) position to "ON" position.
(3) On completion, check that the diagnosis code is set again.
Is the diagnosis code set?
Replace the combination meter (Refer to GROUP 54A - Combination Meter ).
A poor connection, open circuit or other intermittent malfunction is present in the CAN bus lines between the combination meter and the gateway-ECU (for BSW) (Refer to GROUP 00 - How to Cope with Intermittent Malfunctions ).
 
STEP 4. Check whether the diagnosis code is set again.
Check again if the diagnosis code is set in the gateway-ECU (for BSW).
(1) Erase the diagnosis code.
(2) Turn the ignition switch from "LOCK" (OFF) position to "ON" position.
(3) On completion, check that the diagnosis code is not set again.
Is the diagnosis code set?
Replace the gateway-ECU (for BSW) (Refer to ).
A poor connection, open circuit or other intermittent malfunction is present in the CAN bus lines between the combination meter and the gateway-ECU (for BSW) (Refer to GROUP 00 - How to Cope with Intermittent Malfunctions ).
 
54 -CHASSIS ELECTRICAL > 54C-CONTROLLER AREA NETWORK (CAN) > TROUBLESHOOTING<GATEWAY-ECU (FOR BSW)> > DIAGNOSIS CODE PROCEDURES > CODE No.U1073 BUS-OFF
Code No. U1073: Bus-off (CAN-C)
 
 
caution
  • If diagnosis code No. U1073 is set, be sure to diagnose the CAN bus line.
  • When replacing the ECU, always check that the communication circuit is normal.
 
 
TROUBLE JUDGEMENT
When gateway-ECU (for BSW) has ceased the CAN (CAN-C) communication (bus off), code No. U1073 is set.
 
 
PROBABLE CAUSES
  • Malfunction of CAN bus line
  • Malfunction of the gateway-ECU (for BSW)
  • ECU malfunction of other system
54 -CHASSIS ELECTRICAL > 54C-CONTROLLER AREA NETWORK (CAN) > TROUBLESHOOTING<GATEWAY-ECU (FOR BSW)> > DIAGNOSIS CODE PROCEDURES > CODE No.U1190 NO RECEIVE FAULT DETECT SIGNAL
Code No. U1190: No receive fault detect signal
 
 
caution
  • If diagnosis code No. U1190 is set, be sure to diagnose the CAN bus line.
  • When replacing the ECU, always check that the communication circuit is normal.
 
 
JUDGEMENT CRITERIA
ETACS-ECU sends the diagnosis code (U code) detection permission or prohibition signal to each ECU connected to the CAN bus line. If the gateway-ECU (for BSW) cannot receive the diagnosis code (U code) detection permission or prohibition signal for 5 seconds after turning the ignition switch to "ON" position, diagnosis code No. U1190 will be set.
 
 
PROBABLE CAUSES
  • Malfunction of the ETACS-ECU
  • Malfunction of CAN bus line
  • Malfunction of the gateway-ECU (for BSW)
 
 
DIAGNOSIS PROCEDURE
STEP 1. M.U.T.-III CAN bus diagnostics
Use the M.U.T.-III to diagnose the CAN bus lines.
Is the check result normal?
Go to Step 2.
Repair the CAN bus line (Refer to ).
 
STEP 2. M.U.T.-III other system diagnosis code
Check if the diagnosis code is set in the combination meter.
Is the diagnosis code set?
Replace the ETACS-ECU (Refer to GROUP 54A - ETACS ).
Go to Step 3.
 
STEP 3. Diagnosis code recheck
Check again if the diagnosis code is set in the gateway-ECU (for BSW).
(1) Erase the diagnosis code.
(2) Turn the ignition switch from "LOCK" (OFF) position to "ON" position.
(3) Check if the diagnosis code is set.
Is the diagnosis code set?
Replace the gateway-ECU (for BSW) (Refer to ).
Intermittent malfunction is suspected (Refer to GROUP 00 - How to cope with Intermittent Malfunction ).

54 -CHASSIS ELECTRICAL > 54C-CONTROLLER AREA NETWORK (CAN) > TROUBLESHOOTING<GATEWAY-ECU (FOR BSW)> > SYMPTOM CHART

54 -CHASSIS ELECTRICAL > 54C-CONTROLLER AREA NETWORK (CAN) > TROUBLESHOOTING<GATEWAY-ECU (FOR BSW)> > SYMPTOM PROCEDURE > POWER SUPPLY CIRCUIT
Inspection Procedure 1: Power Supply Circuit Check
 
 
 
 
COMMENTS ON TROUBLE SYMPTOM
If the gateway-ECU (for BSW) functions do not work at all, power supply to the gateway-ECU (for BSW), or the gateway-ECU (for BSW) itself may have a problem.
 
 
PROBABLE CAUSES
  • Damaged harness wires and connectors
  • Malfunction of gateway-ECU (for BSW)
 
 
DIAGNOSIS PROCEDURE
STEP 1. Voltage measurement at the gateway-ECU (for BSW) connector
(1) Disconnect the connector, and measure at the wiring harness side.
(2) Turn the ignition switch to the "LOCK" (OFF) position.
(3) Measure the voltage between the gateway-ECU (for BSW) connector (+B terminal) and the body earth.
OK: System voltage
Is the check result normal?
Go to Step 3.
Go to Step 2.
 
STEP 2. Check of open circuit in +B line between the fusible link and gateway-ECU (for BSW) connector
Is the check result normal?
Perform the battery test (Refer to GROUP 54A - Battery, Battery Test ) or check the battery terminals for looseness or contamination.
Repair the connector(s) or wiring harness.
 
STEP 3. Voltage measurement at the gateway-ECU (for BSW) connector
(1) Disconnect the connector, and measure at the wiring harness side.
(2) Turn the ignition switch to the "ON" position.
(3) Measure the voltage between the gateway-ECU (for BSW) connector (IG terminal) and the body earth.
OK: System voltage
Is the check result normal?
Go to Step 6.
Go to Step 4.
 
STEP 4. M.U.T.-III other system data list
Check the input signal from the ignition switch (IG1) in the ETACS-ECU.
  • Turn the ignition switch to the "ON" position.
 
Item No.Item nameNormal condition
30IG SW (IG1)ON
OK: Normal condition is displayed.
Is the check result normal?
Go to Step 5.
NO : Troubleshoot the ETACS-ECU (Refer to GROUP 54A - ETACS, Inspection Procedure 2 "The ignition switch (IG1) signal is not received." ).
 
STEP 5. Check of open circuit in IG line between the ignition switch (IG1) and gateway-ECU (for BSW) connector
Is the check result normal?
The trouble can be an intermittent malfunction (Refer to GROUP 00 - How to Cope with Intermittent Malfunction ).
Repair the connector(s) or wiring harness.
 
STEP 6. Resistance measurement at the gateway-ECU (for BSW) connector
(1) Disconnect the connector, and measure at the wiring harness side.
(2) Measure the resistance between the gateway-ECU (for BSW) connector (GND terminal) and the body earth.
OK: Continuity exists (2 Ω or less)
Is the check result normal?
Go to Step 8.
Go to Step 7.
 
STEP 7. Check of open circuit in GND line between gateway-ECU (for BSW) connector and body earth
Is the check result normal?
The trouble can be an intermittent malfunction (Refer to GROUP 00 - How to Cope with Intermittent Malfunction ).
Repair the connector(s) or wiring harness.
 
STEP 8. Retest the system.
Is the check result normal?
The trouble can be an intermittent malfunction (Refer to GROUP 00 - How to Cope with Intermittent Malfunction ).
Replace the gateway-ECU (for BSW) (Refer to ).

54 -CHASSIS ELECTRICAL > 54C-CONTROLLER AREA NETWORK (CAN) > TROUBLESHOOTING<GATEWAY-ECU (FOR BSW)> > INPUT SIGNAL PROCEDURE > THE BLIND SPOT WARNING SWITCH SIGNAL IS NOT.
Inspection Procedure 1: The blind spot warning switch signal is not received.
 
 
cautionWhenever the ECU is replaced, ensure that the input signal circuit is normal.
 
 
COMMENTS ON TROUBLE SYMPTOM
If there is an error to the blind spot warning switch input signal, the blind spot warning switch signal is no longer output to the communication line.
 
 
PROBABLE CAUSES
  • Malfunction of blind spot warning switch
  • Malfunction of the gateway-ECU (for BSW)
  • Damaged harness wires and connectors
 
 
DIAGNOSIS PROCEDURE
STEP 1. M.U.T.-III data list
Check the input signals from the blind spot warning switch.
  • Operate the blind spot warning switch.
 
Item No.Item nameNormal condition
5BSW SWOFF to ON (only when switch is operated)
OK: Normal condition is displayed.
Is the check result normal?
Go to Step 3.
Go to Step 2.
 
STEP 2. Check of short to earth, and open circuit in DI05 line between the gateway-ECU (for BSW) and blind spot warning switch connector
Is the check result normal?
Go to Step 3.
Repair the wiring harness.
 
STEP 3. Check of open circuit between blind spot warning switch connector earth terminal and body earth
Is the check result normal?
Go to Step 4.
Repair the wiring harness.
 
STEP 4. Check the blind spot warning switch.
Refer to GROUP 54A - Blind spot warning switch, Blind spot warning switch inspection .
Is the check result normal?
Go to Step 5.
Replace the blind spot warning switch (Refer to GROUP 54A - Blind spot warning switch ).
 
STEP 5. M.U.T.-III data list
Check the input signals from the blind spot warning switch.
  • Operate the blind spot warning switch.
 
Item No.Item nameNormal condition
5BSW SWOFF to ON (only when switch is operated)
OK: Normal condition is displayed.
Is the check result normal?
The trouble can be an intermittent malfunction (Refer to GROUP 00 - How to Cope with Intermittent Malfunction ).
Replace the gateway-ECU (for BSW) (Refer to ).
